< text>
Such a gem tucked away in the south west corner or San Diego (and the United States!). You can bunnies, lizards, and all types of birds! There are trails that are beginner friendly (and mostly stroller friendly too). The visitor center is pretty cool (before it got closed for Covid). The estuary is full of beautiful views and it is a great place for a walk or hike (or run). With the benches located along or at the ends of trails, it makes for a nice snack or picnic spot too.< /text>

Alisha Aceituno< /name>

<rate>2<//rate>< Review>
I have played moorpark several times and it usually has been a good experience, although I think they should be more peace officer friendly for those who serve and protect.  It would be nice if they gave us a discount all week and not just monday thru thursday.
Yesterday my collegues and I had a miserable experience at moorpark.  The pace of play was really slow and the condition of the greens were poor, being way too soft with several deep ball marks on every hole.
It was a very hot day so staying hydrated was key.  Unfortuneately, we saw the cart girl once early in our round.  And when we did see her she was extreamly rude.
Then there was our cart.  It didn't have a lot of power to begin with and by the 11th or 12th hole it began to die.  We notified the pro shop of our situation via the 'request for a new cart' botton on the cart.  All of our requests were ignored as nobody came to our rescue.  Being that the course, spread out with a lot of hills, you can imagine how difficult and frustrating it was to complete our round.
After we finished we went to the pro shop to explain what had happend.  We first spoke to the guy behind the counter.  He was very rude and pretty much blew us off, but he did say, "there's nothing I can do, I just work here".  I then asked to speek with his supervisor.  The head pro came out and he was just as rude.
I again explianed the situation.  Instead of appologizing, he began to question my story, making it seem that I was making it all up and all that wanted was a free round or something.  I have never experienced such unporfessionalism at a golf course.  This was extremely disapporinting for my collegues and myself........<//Review>

This place makes a really good mangonada. Very good paleteria. It was very busy when we went, but that's a really good indicator that this place is really good.

They have a really extensive range of ice cream flavors and have a good menu of snacks. I got the elote on a stick, and a large mangonada but would want to try other stuff too like tostilocos and other loaded chips.

The only downside, which isn't the store's fault, is.... the parking sucks. We had to park a couple of blocks down to get to the shop. BUT, that shouldn't stop you from getting good Mexican treats and ice cream from this place!<//Text>

(Translated by Google) In general, a good place for snacks "I suggest the owner pay attention to two details that we observed in our recent visit with the family.
1. The chicharrones prepared very well served and with good presentation.
However, we ordered 3 and the 3 tasted expired (that is, old) we could feel on our palate the taste of the expired oil in the pork rind, and that incidentally was very thin and breaks easily when biting.
I think it can be improved with better quality pork rinds, it is difficult to imagine that a traveling business serves better quality pork rinds (I have been able to verify it) the price would not be an impediment for most of the people and would be more in line with the invetity of this deal.
2. We also asked for 3 ears of corn, but under the preparation, mayonnaise, cheese and chili there were still the corn hairs, which when biting into it was quite unpleasant as they got tangled between our teeth and you had to remove them from your mouth; It seems that no care is really taken to stir them as much as possible before preparing them. I can understand the fact that you need to serve the customer quickly, but just as speed is important, so quality and the final presentation of the product are necessary to ensure that customers return.
We tried the water of mamey oh ... excellent as few.
Parking will be a factor depending on the time you visit the place, in the afternoons it seems to be more complicated.
